decribe an oil painting of a majestic yew tree stands in the middle of an overgrown, wild garden. A barely paved path winds its way through the untamed greenery, leading to the tree. Beneath its shade, a young blonde woman with long braids and a white flower in her hair, wearing a very short red dotted summer dress, is dancing. In the background, a crumbling house adds to the sense of abandonment. The soft light of late afternoon bathes the scene, creating an ethereal and tranquil atmosphere, with a dreamlike quality. low angle
